[05/16/2022 6:10 AM] SThMan#0000
Forwarded from unknown: Think about any product/goods you can see in your life, there are two types of prices.
 
1/ Production cost price: It is the root value of the product. Factories take time/energy/labor/materials... to complete a product then they just sell to commercial/trading companies. This is normally fixed and does not change in a long period. 
 
2/ Market price: It is the result that commercial/trading companies just sell to end-users. Depending on the types of products, the market price can change frequently.
In terms of Bitcoin, which is called a New Gold or a new Ponzi or whatever...
What are you seeing in Binance or Coinbase or CME ... is Market Price. In this market, the volatility is big. Everyone here knows it is manipulated with the combination of Fear/Fomo, Liquidity, Fud/Good News/ Futures/ Leverage manipulation... You are a trader. You work like commercial/trading companies, also you are an end-user. Market price fluctuation can give you profit or loss.
So, what is the root value of Bitcoin?
Key words: Mining Industry/ Miners/ Electricity cost/ Production cost...
Bitcoin is a product. The production cost does not change much in a cycle.  After each halving, difficulty increases, production cost will increase. That makes bitcoin special/valuable in long run.
Market price fluctuate frequently. In a cycle, Bear or bull, It tends to approach the value of production costs. No Miners, No bitcoin. This is the root value of this product. 
For current context in this cycle, 
Electricity cost is 20k (Electricity only)
Production cost is 29-34k ( total cost of electricity/labor/factory..)

[05/16/2022 6:10 AM] SThMan#0000
Forwarded from unknown: If you buy btc below production cost, It can say you buy cheap BTC. In history of Bitcoin, there are only 3 times BTC touched below production cost.
Buying below production cost => Investing
Buying above production cost => Trading

Forwarded from unknown: Understanding this info is really important if you are crypto traders.
There are so much noise like wars, covid, China banning .... that can affect in small time frame price movement but not many people understand the big picture or key points in this space.

[10/20/2022 4:56 AM] manhtunguyen73#0000
Forwarded from ErgoBridgeBot: <mhs_sam> Rosen Bridge:
- still dealing with soft launch. progressing as planned till now.
- Ergo and Cardano wallets integrated into UI.
- there was a p2p connection issue; now we have found the causation and working on the fix.

Introducing ErgoWell:
- after discussions regarding staking Erg in this forum post:
https://www.ergoforum.org/t/sponsored-staking-of-erg/3945/13
we found out that Option3 (see the post) is a viable option.
- ErgoWell is an attempt to provide a venture funding experiment to Ergo.
- It's based on ProfitSharing dapp and has some similarities with ErgoRaffle.
- Based on ErgoWell, anyone can create a fund and propose some yield for the stakers.
- Users can see the fund's properties and assess their risk in order to invest.
- Tokens in the fund's pool can be completely locked (100% locked) or completely liquid (0% locked) or any combination. 
- the liquid funds will be provided to project creator in order to accomplish his specified task and provide additional eventual yield for the stakers.
- fund creator can put some money in the yield pot to provide fixed yield to stakers.
- fund creator can lock some tokens in a collateral pot in order to compensate stakers in the event of default. 

The overall design of ErgoWell is done but contracts are not implemented yet. Open for everyone to jump in. 
Doc will be published in a few days.

{Embed}
https://www.ergoforum.org/t/sponsored-staking-of-erg/3945/13
